<script>
(function () {
  var ga_registrado = true;
  var styleid = 9;
  var analyticsLoaded = false;

  function loadAnalytics() {
    if (analyticsLoaded) return;
    analyticsLoaded = true;
    var script = document.createElement('script');
    script.async = true;
    script.src = 'https://www.googletagmanager.com/gtag/js?id=G-QCY7DPM9MZ';
    script.onload = function () {
      window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
      function gtag(){dataLayer.push(arguments);}
      window.gtag = gtag;
      gtag('js', new Date());
      gtag('config', 'G-QCY7DPM9MZ', {
        is_registered: ga_registrado,
        style_id: styleid
      });
    };
    document.head.appendChild(script);
  }

  function waitForTcfapi(maxWait, interval) {
    var waited = 0;
    function checkTcfapi() {
      if (typeof window.__tcfapi === "function") {
        window.__tcfapi('addEventListener', 2, function (tcData, success) {
          if (success && (tcData.eventStatus === 'tcloaded' || tcData.eventStatus === 'useractioncomplete')) {
            var analyticsConsent =
              tcData.purpose && tcData.purpose.consents && tcData.purpose.consents["10"];
            if (analyticsConsent) loadAnalytics();
          }
        });
      } else if (waited < maxWait) {
        waited += interval;
        setTimeout(checkTcfapi, interval);
      }
    }
    checkTcfapi();
  }

  waitForTcfapi(10000, 250);
})();
</script>

<script>
    //Este script hace un preload del tema para evitar flickering. Es una versión simplificada de la funcion onLoad() que se
    //ejecuta despues.
    const LS_KEYS = {
        FORCE_DARK_MODE: "FORCE_DARK_MODE",
        FORCE_LIGHT_MODE: "FORCE_LIGHT_MODE",
        AUTO_DARK_MODE: "AUTO_DARK_MODE"
    }

    function setDarkMode(set) {
        if (set) {
            document.body.classList.add("dark_theme");
            if (document.querySelector('meta[name="twitter:widgets:theme"]')) {
                document.querySelector('meta[name="twitter:widgets:theme"]').setAttribute("content", 'dark');
            }


        }
        else {
            document.body.classList.remove("dark_theme");
            if (document.querySelector('meta[name="twitter:widgets:theme"]')) {
                document.querySelector('meta[name="twitter:widgets:theme"]').setAttribute("content", 'white');
            }
        }
    }

    function setAutoDarkMode() {
        let matched = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
        if (matched) {
            setDarkMode(true);
        }
        else {
            setDarkMode(false);
        }
    }

    if (localStorage.getItem(LS_KEYS.FORCE_DARK_MODE)) {
        setDarkMode(true);
    }
    if (localStorage.getItem(LS_KEYS.FORCE_LIGHT_MODE)) {
        setDarkMode(false);
    }
    if (localStorage.getItem(LS_KEYS.AUTO_DARK_MODE)) {
        setAutoDarkMode();
    }

</script>

                        window.onload = initShowthreadSearch;
                        function initShowthreadSearch() {
                            checkClearButton();
                            changeSearchParams(10628865);
                        }
                        function checkClearButton() {
                            const input = document.getElementById("searchfield");
                            if (input.value) {
                                document.getElementById("searchfield-clear-wrapper").style.display = 'flex';
                            }
                            else {
                                document.getElementById("searchfield-clear-wrapper").style.display = 'none';
                            }
                        }

                        function resetSearch() {
                            const input = document.getElementById("searchfield");
                            document.getElementById('searchfield-clear-wrapper').style.display = 'none';
                            input.value = ''
                        }


                        initShowthreadSearch()
                    </script>

                <script>

                    function setOnlineStatus() {
                        const switchEl = $("#cb_invisible")[0];
                        $('[name="options[invisible]"]').val(switchEl.checked)
                        $.ajax({
                            type: "POST",
                            url: "profile.php?do=setonlinestatus",
                            data: $("#invisibleform").serialize(),
                            success: function (success, status, xhr) {
                                if (switchEl.checked) {
                                    document.getElementById("user-online-status").style.display = "block"
                                } else {
                                    document.getElementById("user-online-status").style.display = "none"
                                }
                            },
                            error: function (error) {
                                console.error(error);
                                switchEl.checked = !switchEl.checked;
                                if (switchEl.checked) {
                                    document.getElementById("user-online-status").style.display = "block"
                                } else {
                                    document.getElementById("user-online-status").style.display = "none"
                                }
                            }
                        })
                    }
                </script>
            </div>
        </form>

        <script>
            function toogleSubheaderContent() {
                const subheader = document.getElementById("subheader");
                const subheaderContent = document.getElementById("subheader-content");
                const subheaderHide = document.getElementById("subheader-hide");
                if (subheaderHide.classList.contains("expand")) {
                    subheaderContent.style.display = "flex";
                    subheaderHide.classList.remove("expand");
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        subheaderContent.style.transform = "none";
                        setTimeout(() => {
                            subheader.classList.toggle("with-shadow");
                        }, 270)
                    }, 10);
                } else {
                    const subheaderContentFilterButton = document.getElementById('subheader-content-filter-button');
                    const subheaderContentActionButton = document.getElementById('subheader-content-action-button');
                    const subheaderContentWrapperLeftPhone = document.getElementsByClassName('subheader-content-wrapper-left-phone')[0];
                    const subheaderContentWrapperRightPhone = document.getElementsByClassName('subheader-content-wrapper-right-phone')[0];
                    subheaderContent.style.transform = "translateY(-50px)";
                    subheaderHide.classList.add("expand");
                    subheaderContentWrapperLeftPhone.classList.remove('show');
                    subheaderContentFilterButton.classList.remove('active');
                    subheaderContentWrapperRightPhone.classList.remove('show');
                    subheaderContentActionButton.classList.remove('active');
                    subheader.classList.toggle("with-shadow");
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        subheaderContent.style.display = "none";
                    }, 200);
                }
            }


        </script>

        <div id="subheader-content" class="subheader-content">

                <button style="width: 100%;" class="subheader-hide-phone" onclick="onClickFilterActionButtons('filter')">
                    <div id="subheader-content-filter-button" class="subheader-content-filter-button">
                        <span class="subheader-content-button">Filtros</span>
                        <span class="select-chevron"></span>
                    </div>
                </button>

            <script>
                function onClickFilterActionButtons(type) {

                    const subheaderContentFilterButton = document.getElementById('subheader-content-filter-button');
                    const subheaderContentActionButton = document.getElementById('subheader-content-action-button');
                    const subheaderContentWrapperLeftPhone = document.getElementsByClassName('subheader-content-wrapper-left-phone')[0];
                    const subheaderContentWrapperRightPhone = document.getElementsByClassName('subheader-content-wrapper-right-phone')[0];

                    if (type === "filter") {
                        subheaderContentWrapperLeftPhone.classList.toggle('show');
                        subheaderContentWrapperRightPhone.classList.remove('show');
                        subheaderContentFilterButton.classList.toggle('active');
                        subheaderContentActionButton.classList.remove('active');
                    }
                    else {
                        subheaderContentWrapperRightPhone.classList.toggle('show');
                        subheaderContentWrapperLeftPhone.classList.remove('show');
                        subheaderContentActionButton.classList.toggle('active');
                        subheaderContentFilterButton.classList.remove('active');
                    }
                }
                </script>

                <button style="width: 100%;" class="subheader-hide-phone"  onclick="onClickFilterActionButtons('actions')">
                    <div class="subheader-content-filter-button" id="subheader-content-action-button">
                        <span class="subheader-content-button">Acciones</span>
                        <span class="select-chevron"></span>
                    </div>
                </button>

<script>
    function addText(text1,text2,entrada){
        var TheTextBox = document.getElementById("vB_Editor_QR_textarea");
        var entrada = prompt(entrada)

        if (entrada === "") {
            // user pressed OK, but the input field was empty
            TheTextBox.value = TheTextBox.value + text1 + text2;
        } else if (entrada) {
            // user typed something and hit OK
            TheTextBox.value = TheTextBox.value + text1 + entrada + text2;
        } else {
            // user hit cancel
            // TheTextBox.value = TheTextBox.value + text1 + entrada + text2;
        }

    }
</script>

                                <script>
                                        $("#fileToUpload").change(function() {
                                            var formData = new FormData(document.getElementById("qrform"));

                                            var sendFormData = new FormData();

                                            var files = $('#fileToUpload')[0].files;
                                            if (files.length > 0) {
                                                const uploadingActivity = document.getElementById("uploadImageButton");
                                                uploadingActivity.classList.add("uploading");
                                                sendFormData.append("image", files[0]);
                                                sendFormData.append("securitytoken", "1773248403-56941f9fad50389c548a3e0022b16c4954015f44");
                                                $.ajax({
                                                    url: "/foro/image_uploader.php",
                                                    type: "post",
                                                    data: formData,
                                                    dataType: "json",
                                                    processData: false,
                                                    contentType: false
                                                })
                                                    .done(function (res) {
                                                        uploadingActivity.classList.remove("uploading");
                                                        if (!res.success) {
                                                            alert("Ha habido un error cargando la imagen, vuelva a intentarlo");
                                                            return;
                                                        }
                                                        var editor = vB_Editor['vB_Editor_QR'];
                                                        editor.check_focus();
                                                        editor.apply_format("insertimage", false, res.link);
                                                    })
                                                    .error(function (res) {
                                                        uploadingActivity.classList.remove("uploading");
                                                        alert("Ha habido un error cargando la imagen, vuelva a intentarlo");
                                                    });

                                        }
                                        });
                                </script>
                            </label>

    <script>
        function lazyLoadTweets() {
            if (!twttr.widgets) {
                setTimeout(function(){
                    lazyLoadTweets();
                }, 1000);
                return
            }
            var tweets = document.getElementsByClassName("twitter-tweet");
            // if is a tweet is visible load it
            for (const tweet of tweets) {
                //if the user is seeing the tweet load it
                if (tweet.getBoundingClientRect().top -1000 < window.innerHeight
                    && tweet.getBoundingClientRect().bottom + 1500 > window.innerHeight) {
                    twttr.widgets.load(tweet);
                }
            }
        }

        lazyLoadTweets();

        window.addEventListener('load', function () {
            setTimeout(function(){
                lazyLoadTweets();
            }, 1000);
        })
        window.onscroll = lazyLoadTweets;

    </script>

    <script>
        function onLoad() {
            setTimeout(() => {
                if (document.body.scrollIntoView && (window.location.href.indexOf('#') == -1 || window.location.href.indexOf('#post') > -1)) {
                    if (!fetch_object('currentPost')) return;
                    fetch_object('currentPost').scrollIntoView(true);
                }
            }, 600);

            const setSpoilersTextColor = () => {
                const spoilers = document.getElementsByClassName("spoiler")
                for (let i = 0; i < spoilers.length; i++) {
                    if (document.body.classList.contains("dark_theme")) {
                        spoilers[i].onclick = null;
                        spoilers[i].addEventListener("click", () => {
                            spoilers[i].style.color = "var(--text-color)";
                        })
                    }
                }
            }

            function closeGallery() {
                let gallery = document.getElementsByClassName('lightbox')

                    gallery[0].classList.remove('lightbox-visible')
                setTimeout(() => {
                    gallery[0].classList.remove('lightbox-display-visible')
                }, 150);
            }

            function setupLightbox () {

                let images = document.getElementsByClassName('imgpost');
                const imagesLength = images.length;

                if (imagesLength < 0) return;

                let newElement = document.createElement('div')
                newElement.classList.add('lightbox')
                document.body.appendChild(newElement);

                for (let i = 0; i < imagesLength; i++) {

                    function closeCurrentLightbox() {
                        closeGallery()
                    }

                    newElement.onclick = closeCurrentLightbox;

                    let org_html = images[i].outerHTML;

                    images[i].onclick = function() {
                        newElement.innerHTML = '<div class="lightbox-container">' +
                            '<div style="display: flex; flex-direction: column; text-align: right">' +
                            '<div class="lightbox-close-button" onclick="closeGallery()"><p style="color: white">X</p></div>'+
                            org_html +
                            '</div></div>';
                        newElement.classList.add("lightbox-display-visible")
                        setTimeout(() => {
                            newElement.classList.add("lightbox-visible")
                        }, 20);
                    }

                }

            }
            setSpoilersTextColor()
            setupLightbox()

            setTimeout(() => {
                checkTextContrast();
            }, 300);

        }

        function getElementsStartsWithId( parent, id ) {
            var children = parent.getElementsByTagName('*');
            var elements = [], child;
            for (var i = 0, length = children.length; i < length; i++) {
                child = children[i];
                if (child.id.substr(0, id.length) === id)
                    elements.push(child);
            }
            return elements;
        }

        function checkTextContrast() {
            const postbitWrappers = document.getElementsByClassName("postbit_wrapper");
            for (var j = 0; j < postbitWrappers.length; j++) {
                const messages = getElementsStartsWithId(postbitWrappers[j], "post_message_");
                messages.forEach(message => {
                    var elements = message.getElementsByTagName("*");
                    for (var i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) {
                        const elementStyle = elements[i].getAttribute("style");
                        if (elementStyle) {
                            if (elementStyle.includes("color")) {
                                elements[i].removeAttribute("style");
                            }
                        }
                        const elementColor = elements[i].getAttribute("color");
                        if (elementColor) {
                            const fontColor = elementColor;

                            const whiteBackground = [255, 255, 255];
                            const darkBackground = [42, 42, 42];

                            if (contrast(fontColor, whiteBackground) < 2 || contrast(fontColor, darkBackground) < 2) {
                                elements[i].removeAttribute("color");
                            }
                        }
                        const elementFace = elements[i].getAttribute("face");
                        if (elementFace) {
                            elements[i].removeAttribute("face");
                        }
                    }
                })
            }
        }

        document.onload = onLoad();


    </script>

</main>

<script>
    document.addEventListener('scroll', function(e) {
        const link = document.getElementById("scrollToTopButton" );
        if (window.scrollY > 100) {
            link.style.visibility = "visible";
            link.style.opacity = 1;
            link.style.bottom = null;
        }
        else {
            link.style.visibility = "hidden"
            link.style.opacity = 0;
            link.style.bottom = null;
        }
        if (window.innerHeight + window.scrollY >= document.body.scrollHeight - 12) {
            link.style.bottom = "50px";
        }
    })
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    function toggleUserMenu() {
        document.getElementById("user-profile-menu-background").classList.toggle("hidden")
        document.getElementById("user-profile-menu").classList.toggle("hidden")
        if (document.getElementById("user-profile-menu").classList.contains("hidden")) {
            lockBodyScroll(false);
        }
        else {
            lockBodyScroll(true)
        }
    }
    function setDarkMode(set) {
        document.body.classList.add("transition-03");
        if (set) {
            document.body.classList.add("dark_theme");
            document.getElementById("selector-noche").classList.add("active")
            document.getElementById("selector-dia").classList.remove("active")
            document.getElementById("selector-auto").classList.remove("active")
            localStorage.removeItem(LS_KEYS.FORCE_LIGHT_MODE)
            localStorage.removeItem(LS_KEYS.AUTO_DARK_MODE)
            localStorage.setItem(LS_KEYS.FORCE_DARK_MODE, true)
        }
        else {
            document.body.classList.remove("dark_theme");
            document.getElementById("selector-dia").classList.add("active")
            document.getElementById("selector-noche").classList.remove("active")
            document.getElementById("selector-auto").classList.remove("active")
            localStorage.removeItem(LS_KEYS.FORCE_DARK_MODE)
            localStorage.removeItem(LS_KEYS.AUTO_DARK_MODE)
            localStorage.setItem(LS_KEYS.FORCE_LIGHT_MODE, true)
        }
        setTimeout(() => document.body.classList.remove("transition-03"), 700)
    }

    function setAutoDarkMode() {
        document.body.classList.add("transition-03");
        let matched = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
        if (matched) {
            document.body.classList.add("dark_theme");
        }
        else {
            document.body.classList.remove("dark_theme");
        }
        document.getElementById("selector-noche").classList.remove("active")
        document.getElementById("selector-dia").classList.remove("active")
        document.getElementById("selector-auto").classList.add("active")
        localStorage.removeItem(LS_KEYS.FORCE_LIGHT_MODE)
        localStorage.removeItem(LS_KEYS.FORCE_DARK_MODE)
        localStorage.setItem(LS_KEYS.AUTO_DARK_MODE, true)
        setTimeout(() => document.body.classList.remove("transition-03"), 700)
    }


    function onLoad() {
        //check darkmode
        if (localStorage.getItem(LS_KEYS.FORCE_DARK_MODE)) {
            setDarkMode(true);
        }
        else if (localStorage.getItem(LS_KEYS.FORCE_LIGHT_MODE)) {
            setDarkMode(false);
        }
        else if (localStorage.getItem(LS_KEYS.AUTO_DARK_MODE)) {
            setAutoDarkMode();
        }
        else {
            setDarkMode(false);
        }
        if (window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').addEventListener !== undefined) {
            window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)')
                .addEventListener('change', event => {
                    if (localStorage.getItem(LS_KEYS.AUTO_DARK_MODE)) {
                        setAutoDarkMode();
                    }
                })
        }
        if (document.getElementById("usercptools")) {
            vbmenu_register("usercptools");
            let userMenuElem = document.getElementById("usercptools");
            userMenuElem.fixed = true;
        }

        if (document.getElementById("notifications")) {
            vbmenu_register("notifications");
            let notifMenuElem = document.getElementById("notifications");
            notifMenuElem.fixed = true;
        }


    }

    function openSettings() {
        document.getElementById("full-window").classList.remove("hidden");
        toggleUserMenu();
        lockBodyScroll(true);
        setHeaderStyle("back", "Ajustes", closeSettings)
        history.pushState(null, null, location.href);
        window.addEventListener("popstate", popstateListener, true);
    }

    function closeSettings() {
        document.getElementById("full-window").classList.add("hidden");
        setHeaderStyle("main");
        lockBodyScroll(false);
        window.removeEventListener("popstate", popstateListener);
    }

    function setOldDesign () {
        let data = {newstyleset: "5", securitytoken: SECURITYTOKEN, s: "", do: 'updatestyleid'};

        var formBody = [];
        for (var property in data) {
            var encodedKey = encodeURIComponent(property);
            var encodedValue = encodeURIComponent(data[property]);
            formBody.push(encodedKey + "=" + encodedValue);
        }
        formBody = formBody.join("&");

        fetch("/foro/profile.php?do=updatestyleid", {
            method: "POST",
            headers: {'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded'},
            body: formBody
        }).then(res => {
            console.log(res);
            window.location.reload();
        });
    }

    function setToastText(text) {
        const toast = document.getElementById("toast");
        if (toast) {
            toast.innerHTML = text;
        }
    }


    function showToast(duration = 3000) {
        const toast = document.getElementById("toast");
        if (toast) {
            toast.classList.add("show");
            setTimeout(() => toast.classList.remove("show"), duration);
            setTimeout(() => toast.innerHTML = "", duration+1000);
        }
    }

    function copyToClipboard(string, toastText = "Copiado al portapapeles") {
        navigator.clipboard.writeText(string)
        setToastText(toastText);
        showToast();
    }

    function log_out()
    {
        ht = document.getElementsByTagName("html");
        ht[0].style.filter = "progid:DXImageTransform.Microsoft.BasicImage(grayscale=1)";
        if (confirm('¿Realmente quieres finalizar tu sesión?\n\nsi es así, presiona OK si no,\nentonces  presiona el botón CANCEL'))
        {
            return true;
        }
        else
        {
            ht[0].style.filter = "";
            return false;
        }
    }


    function hexToRgb(color) {
        var result = /^#?([a-f\d]{2})([a-f\d]{2})([a-f\d]{2})$/i.exec(color);
        return result ? {
            r: parseInt(result[1], 16),
            g: parseInt(result[2], 16),
            b: parseInt(result[3], 16)
        } : null;
    }

    function luminance(r, g, b) {
        var a = [r, g, b].map(function(v) {
            v /= 255;
            return v <= 0.03928 ?
                v / 12.92 :
                Math.pow((v + 0.055) / 1.055, 2.4);
        });
        return a[0] * 0.2126 + a[1] * 0.7152 + a[2] * 0.0722;
    }

    function contrast(rgb1, rgb2) {

        if (rgb1.includes("#")) {
            rgb1 = hexToRgb(rgb1);
            if (!rgb1) return 0;
            rgb1[0] = rgb1.r;
            rgb1[1] = rgb1.g;
            rgb1[2] = rgb1.b;
        }
        if (rgb2.includes("#")) {
            rgb2 = hexToRgb(rgb2);
            if (!rgb2) return 0;
            rgb2[0] = rgb2.r;
            rgb2[1] = rgb2.g;
            rgb2[2] = rgb2.b;
        }

        var lum1 = luminance(rgb1[0], rgb1[1], rgb1[2]);
        var lum2 = luminance(rgb2[0], rgb2[1], rgb2[2]);
        var brightest = Math.max(lum1, lum2);
        var darkest = Math.min(lum1, lum2);
        return (brightest + 0.05) /
            (darkest + 0.05);
    }

    function toggleSearchHeaderMenu() {
        document.getElementById("search-header-menu").classList.toggle("hidden")
        document.getElementById("usercptools").classList.toggle("hidden")
        document.getElementById("subheader").classList.toggle("hidden")
        document.getElementsByClassName("header-search-icon")[0].classList.toggle("hidden")
        document.getElementsByClassName("header-showthread-info")[0].classList.toggle("hidden")
        document.getElementById("notifications-header-buttons").classList.toggle("hidden")
        if (!document.getElementById("search-header-menu").classList.contains("hidden")) {
            document.getElementById("header").style.height = "auto";
            document.getElementById("header").style.gap = "0";
        }
        else {
            document.getElementById("header").style.height = "";
            document.getElementById("header").style.gap = "var(--gap)";
        }
    }

</script>

        //autotz
        const momObj = moment();
        const newUtcOffset = momObj.utcOffset()
        var utcOffsetHours = 0;
        if (newUtcOffset !== 0) {
            utcOffsetHours = newUtcOffset / 60;
            if (momObj.isDST()) {
                utcOffsetHours -= 1;
            }
        }

        let data = {timezoneoffset: utcOffsetHours, securitytoken: SECURITYTOKEN, s: "", do: 'updatetimezoneoptions', dst: 2};

        var formBody = [];
        for (var property in data) {
            var encodedKey = encodeURIComponent(property);
            var encodedValue = encodeURIComponent(data[property]);
            formBody.push(encodedKey + "=" + encodedValue);

        formBody = formBody.join("&");

        fetch("/foro/profile.php?do=updatetimezoneoptions", {
            method: "POST",

            body: formBody
        }).then(res => {
